# Match 123

Winner: Player 1

# The game begins

:::details Player 1 commits their commands
* **1**: Play card 1 - [legendary] Spawns **38** plane(s) of the **fighter** kind (When killed, increases **AP** by 5 to 14 random own planes.) (When spawned, increases **MAN** by 3 to this plane.) (When killed, deals 4 damage to 32 random enemy bomber planes.) (When killed, heals for 20 to this plane.) (When killed, increases **MAN** by 2 to all helicopter planes.)
* **2**: Play card 2 - [legendary] Does nothing
* **3**: Play card 3 - [legendary] Spawns **19** plane(s) of the **helicopter** kind (Every turn, heals for 1 to 48 random fighter planes.) (When killed, deals 4 damage to all planes.) (When killed, increases **AP** by 5 to all own planes.) (When spawned, increases **DP** by 1 to 38 random planes.) (When spawned, increases **AP** by 1 to all planes.) (When spawned, increases **DP** by 4 to 13 random enemy helicopter planes.)
* **4**: Play card 4 - [legendary]  When an own plane is killed, increases **AP** by 4 to 47 random helicopter planes.
* **5**: Play card 5 - [legendary] Spawns **68** plane(s) of the **fighter** kind (When killing a target, deals 17 damage to all own helicopter planes.) (When killing a target, heals for 9 to 48 random planes.)
* **6**: Play card 6 - [legendary] Spawns **42** plane(s) of the **bomber** kind (When spawned, increases **MAN** by 3 to 23 random own helicopter planes.) (When killing a target, increases **AP** by 2 to 32 random planes.) (When spawned, increases **DP** by 4 to 5 random enemy bomber planes.) (When killing a target, increases **MAN** by 5 to all own bomber planes.) (When spawned, increases **AP** by 3 to all planes.) (When spawned, increases **AP** by 4 to all enemy bomber planes.)
:::

:::details Player 2 commits their commands
* **1**: Play card 11 - [legendary] Does nothing
* **2**: Play card 12 - [legendary] Spawns **44** plane(s) of the **fighter** kind (When killed, deals 23 damage to all own planes.) (When killing a target, increases **MAN** by 4 to all own helicopter planes.)
* **3**: Play card 13 - [legendary]  When an enemy fighter plane is killed, deals 14 damage to 25 random planes. When an own plane is killed, deals 21 damage to 49 random enemy bomber planes. When an enemy plane is killed, heals for 23 to 17 random planes.
* **4**: Play card 14 - [legendary] Does nothing
* **5**: Play card 15 - [legendary]  When a plane is killed, deals 22 damage to all own helicopter planes. When an enemy plane is killed, increases **MAN** by 5 to 45 random helicopter planes. Every turn, increases **MAN** by 3 to 40 random enemy planes. When an enemy bomber plane is killed, deals 11 damage to all own planes. Once, deals 5 damage to all enemy helicopter planes.
* **6**: Play card 16 - [legendary] Spawns **44** plane(s) of the **bomber** kind
:::

:::details Player 1 adds a card to the playing deck
[legendary] Spawns **38** plane(s) of the **fighter** kind (When killed, increases **AP** by 5 to 14 random own planes.) (When spawned, increases **MAN** by 3 to this plane.) (When killed, deals 4 damage to 32 random enemy bomber planes.) (When killed, heals for 20 to this plane.) (When killed, increases **MAN** by 2 to all helicopter planes.)
:::

## Turn 6 begins

:::::details Player 2 plays a card
[legendary]  When an enemy fighter plane is killed, deals 14 damage to 25 random planes. When an own plane is killed, deals 21 damage to 49 random enemy bomber planes. When an enemy plane is killed, heals for 23 to 17 random planes.
:::::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
When an enemy fighter plane is killed, deals 14 damage to 25 random planes.
:::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
When an own plane is killed, deals 21 damage to 49 random enemy bomber planes.
:::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
When an enemy plane is killed, heals for 23 to 17 random planes.
:::

**The units are shuffled.**

## Turn 8 begins

:::::details Player 1 plays a card
[legendary] Spawns **19** plane(s) of the **helicopter** kind (Every turn, heals for 1 to 48 random fighter planes.) (When killed, deals 4 damage to all planes.) (When killed, increases **AP** by 5 to all own planes.) (When spawned, increases **DP** by 1 to 38 random planes.) (When spawned, increases **AP** by 1 to all planes.) (When spawned, increases **DP** by 4 to 13 random enemy helicopter planes.)

## Turn 9 begins

:::::details Player 2 plays a card
[legendary]  When a plane is killed, deals 22 damage to all own helicopter planes. When an enemy plane is killed, increases **MAN** by 5 to 45 random helicopter planes. Every turn, increases **MAN** by 3 to 40 random enemy planes. When an enemy bomber plane is killed, deals 11 damage to all own planes. Once, deals 5 damage to all enemy helicopter planes.
:::::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
When a plane is killed, deals 22 damage to all own helicopter planes.
:::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
When an enemy plane is killed, increases **MAN** by 5 to 45 random helicopter planes.
:::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
Every turn, increases **MAN** by 3 to 40 random enemy planes.
:::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
When an enemy bomber plane is killed, deals 11 damage to all own planes.
:::

:::details Player 2 activates an effect
Once, deals 5 damage to all enemy helicopter planes.
:::
